"You are so pretty and colorful."The butterfly says:"Thank you, but I do not like to be caught. I like to be free and fly in the garden. The garden is my home. I have many friends here. We are grateful for it."The butterfly says:"It is okay, Lily and Ben. I forgive you. Jax's favorite spot to stretch and yawn is outside in the bright sun. You are nice and curious. We agree. We will be gentle and respectful. We will be your friends."The butterfly smiles. It says:"Thank you, Lily and Ben. You are smart and kind. You make me happy. Come, let us play in the garden. There is so much to see and learn and enjoy."Lily and Ben smile too. They get up and follow the butterfly. They play in the garden. They are happy. Run Jax run!.

Lily touched the button one more time and started her adventure.

She paddled away from the shore.Max ran to their mom and told her what Lily did. Mom was not happy. She said, "Lily, come back here. You have to behave. You have to be nice to your brother. You have to share the kayak." Lily heard mom and felt sorry. She realized she was selfish and mean. She paddled back to the shore and said, "I am sorry, Max. I was wrong. Do you want to paddle the kayak with me?" Max smiled and said, "Yes, I do. Thank you, Lily. I forgive you." They hugged and got into the kayak. They paddled together and had fun. Mom was proud of them. She said, "That is better. You are good twins. I love you both."

Original Story: Sara and Tom were friends who liked to play in the pool. They had fun splashing and swimming and laughing. One day, a new boy came to the pool. His name was Ben and he had a big toy boat. He put his boat in the water and made it go fast.Sara and Tom wanted to see the boat, but Ben did not want to share. He said, "This is my boat, go away!" He pushed Sara and Tom with his boat and made them wet. Sara and Tom felt sad and angry. They said, "That is not nice, Ben. You should share your toys with others."Ben did not listen. He kept playing with his boat and ignored Sara and Tom. He thought he was better than them. He said, "I don't need friends, I have a boat. You are silly and boring."Sara and Tom decided to leave the pool and play somewhere else. They did not want to be with Ben. They found a nice park with swings and slides and flowers. They had fun again and made new friends.Ben stayed in the pool with his boat. He did not have fun. He felt lonely and bored. He wanted to play with Sara and Tom, but they were gone. He looked around and saw no one. He started to cry. He wished he had been nice and shared his boat. He felt ashamed of himself.The moral of the story is: Sharing is caring. If you are selfish and mean, you will lose your friends and be unhappy. If you are generous and kind, you will make friends and be happy.
Original Summary: Sara and Tom enjoyed playing in the pool with their new friend Ben, but Ben's selfishness and refusal to share his toy boat led to him being left out and lonely, while Sara and Tom made new friends in a nearby park. He felt tired and hungry.He came to a clearing, where he saw a house. He hoped to find some food or water there. He walked closer, but he saw a dog. The dog barked at him and chased him. The little deer was afraid and ran back to the forest. He felt hopeless and hurt.He lay down under a bush, and cried. He wished his friends were there. He wished his mom was there. He wished someone would comfort him.Then, he heard a soft voice. It was a girl, who lived in the house. She had seen the dog chase the deer, and she felt sorry for him. He ate and drank, and felt better. He thanked the girl."You're welcome, little deer. I'm glad you're feeling better. What's your name?"The little deer told her his name. She told him hers."My name is Lily. I live in the house with my mom and dad and the dog. The dog is not mean, he just likes to play. He won't bother you anymore. I'll tell him to leave you alone."The little deer smiled. He liked Lily. She was nice and friendly. He felt some comfort and friendship."Thank you, Lily. You are very kind. Can I stay with you for a while? I'm lost and I can't find my friends."Lily nodded. She wanted to help the deer. She wanted to be his friend."Of course, you can stay with me. I'll take care of you. Maybe we can find your friends later. Come on, let's go to the house. I'll show you my room and my toys. We can play together. You'll like it there."The little deer followed Lily to the house. He felt happy and powerful again. He had found a new friend. He had found a new home.

Original Story: One day, a white duck was walking to the pond with her friends. She saw a farmer working in his field. He had a big hat and a shovel. The duck was curious and wanted to talk to him."Hello, farmer!" the duck said. "What are you doing?"The farmer looked up and smiled. "Hello, duck. I am digging holes for my seeds. I want to grow corn and carrots and beans.""That sounds fun," the duck said. "Can I help you?"The farmer shook his head. "No, thank you, duck. You have to go to the pond with your friends. It is time for your swim and your lunch."The duck nodded, but she did not want to leave. She liked the farmer and his field. She decided to delay her swim and her lunch. She stayed with the farmer and watched him dig. She asked him many questions and he answered them kindly.Meanwhile, her friends waited for her at the pond. They were hungry and bored. They wondered where the duck was. They called her name, but she did not hear them. They started to worry. They thought she might be lost or in trouble.After a while, the farmer finished his work. He thanked the duck for her company and told her to go to the pond. He said he had to go to his house and have his lunch.The duck realized she had been gone for a long time. She said goodbye to the farmer and ran to the pond. She hoped her friends were still there.When she got to the pond, she saw her friends. They were angry and sad. They scolded her for being late and for not listening to the farmer. They said she had missed her swim and her lunch. They said they did not want to play with her anymore.The duck felt sorry and ashamed. She had been selfish and rude. She had not cared about her friends. She had only cared about herself. She wished she had not delayed her swim and her lunch. She wished she had followed the farmer's advice.She apologized to her friends and asked them to forgive her. She said she had learned her lesson. She said she would never do it again.Her friends saw that she was sincere and they forgave her. They hugged her and shared their lunch with her. They said they were still her friends and they loved her.The duck was happy and grateful. She thanked her friends and joined them for a swim. She decided to always listen to the farmer and to her friends. She decided to never delay what was important and good.The moral of the story is: Do not delay what is important and good. Listen to those who know better and care for you. Be a good friend and a good listener.

Despite her friends' worries and scolding, Duckie learned the importance of listening to others and not delaying what's important after apologizing and making amends. The moral of the story is to prioritize what's good and important, listen to those who care, and be a good friend and listener.

She knows what they are doing. She walks around the class. She looks at their papers. She sees their jokes and drawings and names. She is very angry. She says they are naughty and lazy. She says they have to stay after school. She says they have to do the work again. And they have to do more work. And they have to say sorry.Tom and Sue are very sad. From that day forward, the boy always listened to his grandpa's advice.

Original Story: Once upon a time, there was a little boy named Timmy. He lived in a house near a big river. One day, it rained a lot and the river started to get bigger and bigger. Timmy looked out the window and saw that the road was very rough because of the rain. Suddenly, the car hit a big bump and Timmy's toy car vanished! The angel helped the soldier get up and heal his wounds. The soldier was very happy and thanked the angel. From that day on, the soldier knew that praying could help him in times of need.
Original Summary: A brave and strong soldier helped people and protected them from danger, but when he got hurt fighting a big monster, he prayed to the stars for help and an angel appeared to heal him. The soldier was grateful and realized that praying could help him in times of need.

He decided to go and see the world.He took the first step and started to stir the world around him. Everywhere he went, he saw trouble. People were fighting and yelling. He didn't understand why they couldn't just be nice to each other. So he kept stirring the world, shaking things up and making people think differently.But then he heard a voice. It was soft and gentle. He looked around and saw a small girl. She wasn't in any trouble, she just wanted to ask him a question. He couldn't hear her but he could feel that she had something important to say.He held his ear up to her and she spoke softly again. She asked him why he was stirring up trouble. He smiled and told her that he wanted to make the world a better place for everyone.The girl smiled so big and hugged him. He hugged her back and from then on, he never stirred up trouble again. He just helped people who needed it.
Original Summary: A deaf man, feeling lonely and disconnected from the world, sets out to explore and make a positive impact. Along the way, he encounters conflict and decides to continue stirring things up, but eventually meets a kind girl who asks him why he's causing trouble. Touched by her concern, he realizes his true purpose is to help those in need and from then on, he focuses on providing aid to those who need it.

She prevented herself from getting sick again. She was a good cat.
